add_namespace = pacific_war
add_namespace = pacific_war_news

country_event = { # USA get notification about peace with JAP
    id = pacific_war.0 #日本提出有条件停火
    title = pacific_war.0.t
    desc = pacific_war.0.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_europe_pact

    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = { # surrender
        name = pacific_war.0.a
        set_global_flag = pw_usa_offer_surrender
        clr_global_flag = pw_usa_refuse_surrender
        hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = pacific_war.1 days = 3 } }
		}
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 10
            modifier = {
                OR = {
                    NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
                    CHI = { is_ally_with = JAP }
                    605 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes }
                }
                add = 10
            }
            modifier = {
                has_navy_size = { size < 100 }
                add = 25
            }
            modifier = {
                ENG = {
                    any_enemy_country = { has_war_with = FROM }
                    has_capitulated = yes
                }
                add = 50
            }
            modifier = {
                SOV = {
                    any_enemy_country = { has_war_with = FROM }
                    has_capitulated = yes
                }
                add = 25
            }
            modifier = {
                any_core_state = {
                    is_controlled_by = JAP
                    is_in_home_area = yes
                }
                factor = 10
            }
        }
    }
    option = { # never
		name = pacific_war.0.b
        set_global_flag = pw_usa_refuse_surrender
        clr_global_flag = pw_usa_offer_surrender
        hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = pacific_war.1 days = 3 } }
		}
        add_war_support = -0.05
        add_stability = -0.05
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 0
        }
    }
}

country_event = { # JAP get response from USA
    id = pacific_war.1 #[get_usa_response_title]
    title = pacific_war.1.t
    desc = pacific_war.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_macarthur_speech

    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = { # USA agrees to surrender
        name = pacific_war.1.a
        trigger = { has_global_flag = pw_usa_offer_surrender }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pw_usa_surrender_tt		
		hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {					
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = USA
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = JAP
						days = 90
					}
				}
	            white_peace = USA				
				every_country = {					
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = ENG
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = JAP
						days = 90
					}
				}				
			JAP = {
			transfer_state = 629
			transfer_state = 638
			transfer_state = 630			
			transfer_state = 631
			transfer_state = 632
			transfer_state = 639			
			transfer_state = 727
			transfer_state = 642
			transfer_state = 643
			transfer_state = 650			
			transfer_state = 725			
            set_autonomy = { target = INS autonomy_state = autonomy_jiaozong freedom_level = 0.50  }
            }
        MAL = {				
	        set_state_controller = 1055
			set_state_owner = 1055
	        set_state_controller =1058
			set_state_owner = 1058
            set_state_controller = 1061
			set_state_owner = 1061
	        set_state_controller = 336
			set_state_owner = 336
	        set_state_controller =1057
			set_state_owner = 1057
            set_state_controller = 1059
			set_state_owner = 1059
	        set_state_controller = 1056
			set_state_owner = 1056
	        set_state_controller =970
			set_state_owner = 970
            set_state_controller = 972
			set_state_owner = 972
		    set_state_controller = 971
			set_state_owner = 971
            set_state_controller = 333
			set_state_owner = 333				
            set_capital = {
                state = 1055
                remember_old_capital = no
            }
	            } 		
            JAP ={
                   set_autonomy = { target = INS autonomy_state = autonomy_jiaozong freedom_level = 0.50  }
            } 
            JAP ={
                   set_autonomy = { target = MAL autonomy_state = autonomy_jiaozong freedom_level = 0.50  }
            } 
            JAP ={
                   set_autonomy = { target = SIA autonomy_state = autonomy_jiaozong freedom_level = 0.50  }
            } 		
            JAP ={			
                        annex_country = { target = PHI }
                        annex_country = { target = BUR }
                        annex_country = { target = FIC }	
            }						
			every_country = { news_event = { id = pacific_war_news.0 days = 3 } }
			pw_jap_scripted_peace = yes
		}
    }
    option = { # USA won't surrender, back to negotiation
        name = pacific_war.1.b
        trigger = { has_global_flag = pw_usa_refuse_surrender }
        clr_country_flag = jap_offer_peace_usa
    }
    } # close pacific_war.1 after second option

        }
	}

    }

        name = pacific_war_news.0.b

    }

    }
    option = {
        name = pacific_war_news.0.e
        trigger = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = JAP has_war_with = JAP } }
    }
}

add_namespace = vnr_pearl_harbor
add_namespace = vnr_pearl_harbor_news
add_namespace = vnr_pearl_harbor_ai

country_event = { # discuss of Pearl Harbor Plan
    id = vnr_pearl_harbor.0 #讨论对[USA.GetName]的预防作战
    title = vnr_pearl_harbor.0.t
    desc = vnr_pearl_harbor.0.d

    trigger = {
        tag = JAP
        date > 1940.6.1
		OR = {
			is_ally_with = CHI
			CHI = {
				all_owned_state = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes }
			}
			date > 1940.12.7
		}
        can_launch_pearl_harbor = yes 
    }
    picture = GFX_vnr_ph_jap_command
    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
    fire_only_once = yes
    option = { # yes
        name = vnr_pearl_harbor.0.a
        set_global_flag = vnr_pearl_harbor_ongoing
        set_country_flag = { flag = ph_preparation value = 0 }
        activate_mission = ph_attack_countdown
        add_political_power = 100
        hidden_effect = {
            set_variable = {
                var = ph_score
                value = 0
            }
            USA = {
                set_variable = { var = anti_ph_score value = 0 }
                activate_mission = ph_keep_pacific_presence
                country_event = vnr_pearl_harbor.8
            }
        }
    }
    option = { # no
        name = vnr_pearl_harbor.0.b
        custom_effect_tooltip = stop_pearl_harbor_tt
        add_war_support = -0.1
        add_political_power = -50
        ai_chance = {
            base = 0
        }
    }
}

            idea = jap_ph_preparation_1

        }
        hidden_effect = {
            modify_country_flag = {
                flag = ph_preparation

            }

        }
    }
}

country_event = { # check USA defense in Pearl Harbor
    id = vnr_pearl_harbor.4

    is_triggered_only = yes
    hidden = yes
    immediate = {
        clr_global_flag = vnr_pearl_harbor_ongoing
        if = {
            limit = {
                USA = {
                    is_ai = no
                    ships_in_state_ports = {
                        type = capital_ship
                        size > 4
                        state = 629
                    }
                }
            }
            country_event = vnr_pearl_harbor.5
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { 
                USA = {
                    is_ai = yes
                    has_navy_size = {
                        size > 4
                        type = capital_ship
                        archetype = ship_hull_heavy
                    }
                }
            }
            country_event = vnr_pearl_harbor.5
        }
        else = {
            country_event = vnr_pearl_harbor.6
        }
    }
}

country_event = { # Nagumo's choice to send the third wave or not
    id = vnr_pearl_harbor.5 #南云的打算
    title = vnr_pearl_harbor.5.t
    desc = vnr_pearl_harbor.5.d
	picture = GFX_vnr_ph_carrier

    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = vnr_pearl_harbor.5.a
        custom_effect_tooltip = ph_retreat_right_now
        set_global_flag = vnr_attack_on_pearl_harbor
        hidden_effect = { 
            if = {
                limit = { has_idea = jap_ph_preparation_3 }
                remove_ideas = jap_ph_preparation_3
            }
            every_country = {
                news_event = { id = vnr_pearl_harbor_news.0 days = 1 }
            }
            add_timed_idea = {
                idea = jap_ph_attack_two_waves
                days = 100
            }
        }
        ai_chance = {
            base = 20
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = vnr_pearl_harbor.5.b
        custom_effect_tooltip = ph_carry_on_attack
        set_global_flag = vnr_attack_on_pearl_harbor
        hidden_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = { has_idea = jap_ph_preparation_3 }
                remove_ideas = jap_ph_preparation_3
            }
        }
        
        random_list = {
            10 = {
                custom_effect_tooltip = ph_third_wave_success
                hidden_effect = { 
                    every_country = {
                        news_event = { id = vnr_pearl_harbor_news.1 days = 1 }
                    }
                    add_timed_idea = {
                        idea = jap_ph_attack_three_waves
                        days = 100
                    }
                }
            }
            40 = {
                custom_effect_tooltip = ph_third_wave_fail
                hidden_effect = { 
                    every_country = {
                        news_event = { id = vnr_pearl_harbor_news.0 days = 1 }
                    }
                    add_timed_idea = {
                        idea = jap_ph_attack_three_waves
                        days = 100
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        ai_chance = {
            base = 2
        }
    }
}

news_event = { # historical victory
    id = vnr_pearl_harbor_news.0 #珍珠港事件

    desc = vnr_pearl_harbor_news.0.d

            damage_building = { type = naval_base damage = 2 }
        }
    }

        name = vnr_pearl_harbor_news.0.b

            add_timed_idea = {
                idea = for_the_emperor_idea
                days = 365

            target = USA
            type = annex_everything

			limit = { is_ai = yes }

						type = infantry_equipment

					}

				        type = train_equipment
				        amount = 100
				        producer = JAP
			        }

						amount = 500
						producer = JAP
					}

						type = anti_tank_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = JAP
					}

					}

news_event = {#guo
    id = pearl.1 #珍珠港遭受攻击

    title = pearl.1.t

    picture = pearl_harbor_us_event

    desc = pearl.1.d
	
    major = yes
	trigger = {	
    has_global_flag = touxi_zhenzhugang
	NOT = {	
    has_global_flag = touxi_zhenzhugang2
    }	
    }	
    immediate = {
	hidden_effect = {
    set_global_flag = touxi_zhenzhugang2	
	JAP = {
	
	        if = {
			limit = {
			PHI = { is_subject_of = USA }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = PHI
					generator = {
					}
				}
				if = {
				limit = {
				PHI = { is_ai = yes }
				}
				division_template = {
		name = "南洋派遣军"
		regiments = {
		            infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }

# Soviets Push Back And Win
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.3 #边境冲突：苏联胜利
	title = rcmjapan.3.t
	desc = rcmjapan.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_soldiers_tank

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			761 = {
				is_owned_by = JAP
				any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SOV } }
			}
			761 = { add_manpower = -30000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					761 = {
						is_owned_by = JAP
						any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SOV }
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SOV } }
				add_manpower = -30000
			}
		}

		army_experience = 5
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = rcmjapan.3.t #test_the_ussr_focus
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = cat_anti_tank
		}
		name = rcmjapan.3.a
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviet.2 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.27
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = JAP_intervene_in_china
		is_subject_of = JAP
		OR = {
			tag = HPC
			tag = EHB
			tag = RFM
		}
		has_country_flag = im_rrc_now
		CHI = { is_puppet_of = JAP }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			annex_country = { target = CHI transfer_troops = yes }
			annex_country = { target = RFM transfer_troops = yes }
			annex_country = { target = EHB transfer_troops = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = JAP
						has_country_flag = im_rrc_now
					}
				}
				annex_country = { target = HPC transfer_troops = yes }
			}
			set_political_party = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 55 }
			set_political_party = { ideology = fascism popularity = 45 }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
			RRC_core = yes
			JAP = { puppet = ROOT }
		}
	}
	option = {}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.30
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		exists = yes
		has_country_flag = im_jnc_now
		has_global_flag = jnc_exists
		OR = {
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 597 }
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 1079 }
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 1077 }
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 1028 }
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 743 }
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 614 }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 597 }
				}
				set_state_controller = 597
			    set_state_owner = 597 ###
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 1079 }
				}
				set_state_controller = 1079
			    set_state_owner = 1079 ###
			}

				}

#puppet transfer states<=JAP/not the right ruler
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.33
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		exists = yes
		OR = {
			JAP = {
				has_completed_focus = JAP_intervene_in_china
			}
			date > 1939.1.1
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {#tag = EHB
				tag = EHB
				has_global_flag = jnc_exists
			}
			AND = {#tag = hpc
				tag = HPC
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
			tag = RFM
			tag = ECA
		}
		is_puppet_of = JAP
		NOT = { has_country_flag = transfer_state_loop }
		num_of_controlled_states > 1
		any_other_country = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
			has_war_with = JAP
			OR = {
				is_originally_warlord = yes
				is_legit_china = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = ROOT.core_states
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_fully_controlled_by = JAP
						controller = {
							is_subject_of = JAP
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ECA
					}
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = { set_state_controller = PREV }
			}
		}
		country_event = { hours = 8 id = rcmjapan.9834 }
	}
	option = {
		set_country_flag = transfer_state_loop
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.633
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_legit_china = yes
			is_warlord = yes
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = transfer_state_loop_chi }
		has_war_with = JAP
		any_neighbor_country = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		any_of_scopes = {				
			array = global.small_china
			tooltip = small_china_tt
			ROOT = {
				has_full_control_of_state = PREV
				NOT = {
					owns_state = PREV
				}
			}
			owner = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.small_china
			tooltip = small_china_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						NOT = {
							owns_state = PREV
						}
					}
					owner = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						is_capital_of_japan_puppet = yes
					}
				}
				#if = {#NO COMMIE MILITIA #this is changed to use on actions
				#	limit = {
				#		NOT = { has_state_flag = commie_ridden_states }
				#		NOT = { has_state_flag = commie_amassed_support } #now they gotta amass support before they can take over it directly
				#	}
				#	add_core_of = ROOT
				#	ROOT = { set_state_owner = PREV }
				#}
				######COMMUNIST TAKE OVER
				if = {#COMMIE MILITIA AMASSED SUPPORT
					limit = {
						#has_state_flag = commie_amassed_support
						is_core_of = event_target:WTT_communist_china
						has_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
					}
					event_target:WTT_communist_china = { transfer_state = PREV }
					clr_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmjapan.634 }
		set_country_flag = transfer_state_loop_chi
	}
	option = {
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.636
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		exists = yes
		OR = {
			JAP = {
				has_completed_focus = JAP_intervene_in_china
			}
			date > 1939.1.1
		}
		AND = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = RFM
				country_exists = EHB
				AND = {
					country_exists = HPC
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = JAP
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = jnc_exists
			}
			tag = JAP
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = transfer_state_loop_jap }
		num_of_controlled_states > 1
		has_war_with = CHI
		NOT = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = JAP.subjects
				is_rrc = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.big_china
			if = {
				limit = {
					controller = {
						is_subject_of = JAP
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
					NOT = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = JAP.subjects
							PREV = {
								OR = {
									is_claimed_by = PREV
									is_core_of = PREV
								}
							}
						}
					}
					owner = {
						has_war_with = JAP
					}
				}
				JAP = { set_state_controller = PREV }
			}
		}
		country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmjapan.635 }
	}
	option = {
		set_country_flag = transfer_state_loop_jap
	}
}
#Expand RRC#
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.34 #扩大我们的傀儡政权？
	title = rcmjapan.34.t
	desc = rcmjapan.34.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_japanese_handshake
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
		NOT = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_warlord = yes
					TAG = PRC
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				EHB = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
				country_exists = EHB
				EHB = { is_neighbor_of = JAP }
			}
			AND = {
				HPC = { is_subject_of = JAP }
				HPC = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
				country_exists = HPC
				HPC = { is_neighbor_of = JAP }
			}
			AND = {
				RFM = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
				country_exists = RFM
				RFM = { is_neighbor_of = JAP }
			}
			AND = {
				621 = {
				   is_owned_by = JAP
				   is_core_of = ECA
			    }
				746 = {
				   is_owned_by = JAP
				   is_core_of = ECA
			    }
				1019 = {
					is_owned_by = JAP
					is_core_of = ECA
				}
				1020 = {
					is_owned_by = JAP
					is_core_of = ECA
				}
			}
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = EHB
				is_core_of = RFM
				is_core_of = ECA
				is_claimed_by = EHB
				is_claimed_by = RFM
				is_claimed_by = ECA
				AND = {
					is_core_of = HPC
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_claimed_by = HPC
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}		
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RRC_expand }
		AND = {
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					OR = {
						is_warlord = yes
						TAG = PRC
					}
					OR = {
						JAP = {
							has_wargoal_against = PREV
						}
						JAP = {
							has_war_with = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = RRC_expand
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.34.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_stability = 0.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = JAP.subjects
						is_rrc = yes
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					OR = {
						is_core_of = EHB
						is_claimed_by = EHB
					}
					NOT = {
						HPC = {
							is_subject_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
				EHB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = JAP
					}
					EHB = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = im_jnc_now
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_core_of = HPC
						is_claimed_by = HPC
					}
				}
				HPC = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					OR = {
						is_core_of = RFM
						is_claimed_by = RFM
					}
				}
				RFM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				EHB = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					OR = {
						is_core_of = EHB
						is_claimed_by = EHB
					}
				}
				EHB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				HPC = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					OR = {
						is_core_of = HPC
						is_claimed_by = HPC
					}
				}
				HPC = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			else = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = JAP
						OR = {
							is_core_of = RFM
							is_claimed_by = RFM
						}
					}
					RFM = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = JAP
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ECA
					is_claimed_by = ECA
				}
			}
			ECA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		country_event = { hours = 3 id = rcmjapan.535 }
		#ECA = { country_event = { hours = 3 id = rcmjapan.736 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.34.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.1
		country_event = { hours = 3 id = rcmjapan.535 }
	}

		}

#emperor's mind
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.47
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = showa_restoration_focus }
		focus_progress = {
			focus = showa_restoration_focus
			progress > 0.2
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		#if = {
		#	limit = {
		#		OR = {
		#			is_historical_focus_on = yes
		#			AND = {
		#				has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
		#				has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
		#			}
		#		}
		#	}
		#	set_country_flag = emperor_refuses
		#}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
					has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
						has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
						has_idea = kanin_kotohito
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { set_country_flag = emperor_refuses }
				25 = { set_global_flag = nothing_here }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
					has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
						has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
					has_idea = kanin_kotohito
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = { set_country_flag = emperor_refuses }
				50 = { set_global_flag = nothing_here }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
						has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
					has_idea = kanin_kotohito
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
						has_idea = kanin_kotohito
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				30 = { set_country_flag = emperor_refuses }
				70 = { set_global_flag = nothing_here }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
						has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
					has_idea = kanin_kotohito
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				0 = { set_country_flag = emperor_refuses }
				100 = { set_global_flag = nothing_here }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
	}
}

		name = rcmjapan.67.a

		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.big_china
			tooltip = big_china_tt
			if = {
				limit = {							
					state_should_be_transferred_to_china = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { JAP = { has_completed_focus = JAP_expand_the_revolutions_focus } }
					event_target:WTT_communist_china = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { JAP = { NOT = {  has_completed_focus = JAP_expand_the_revolutions_focus } } }
					event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { hours = 5 id = rcmjapan.69 }
		}
	}
}

#the creation of MEN (ACCEPT, 1st time)
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.984
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { #so china and SHX get to keep what they captured
			if = {
				limit = {
					PLM = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = CHI
							has_war_with = SHX
						}						
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							PLM = {
								controls_state = 1014
							}
						}
					}
					SHX = {
						transfer_state = 1014
						transfer_state = 621
						transfer_state = 746
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							PLM = {
								AND = { 
									controls_state = 621
								    controls_state = 746 
							    }
							}
						}
					}
					SHX = {
						transfer_state = 621
						transfer_state = 746
					}
				}			
			}
		}
		PLM = {
			every_unit_leader = {
			    set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = PLM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		MEN_CREATION = yes
	}
	option = {
	}
}

	title = rcmjapan.1002.t

	picture = GFX_report_event_MAN_official

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		is_subject = no
		328 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
			#is_owned_by = JAP
		}
		NOT = {
			country_exists = MAN
		}
		NOT = {#I don't want event pops-up
			has_country_flag = no_rebuild_MAN
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = MAN_no_more
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {#YES
		name = rcmjapan.1002.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		MAN = {
			transfer_state = 328
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_manchuria_state = yes
				}
				add_core_of = MAN
			}
			army_experience = 25
			puppet_reclaim_land = yes
		}
		puppet = MAN
		hidden_effect = {
			MAN = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 30
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = n_socialism
					popularity = 0
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 70
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				MAN = {
					event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
						PREV = {
							add_to_war = {
								targeted_alliance = JAP
								enemy = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#option = {#NO
	#	name = rcmjapan.1002.b
	#}
	option = {#NO FOREVER
		name = rcmjapan.1002.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = no_rebuild_MAN
	}
}

	title = rcmjapan.1003.t

	picture = GFX_report_event_EHB_council

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP

			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
			#is_owned_by = JAP
			NOT = {
				is_owned_by = HPC
				HPC = {
					is_subject_of = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {#got sabotaged
			country_exists = EHB
		}
		NOT = {#I don't want event pops-up
			has_country_flag = no_rebuild_EHB
		}
		NOT = {#has not transformed into prov gov yet

		}

	}

			factor = 100
		}

		}

		}
		OR = {

				country_exists = EHB
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = EHB
				EHB = {
					NOT = {
						owns_state = 608
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = no_rebuild_JNC
		}
		#EHB has transformed

			has_global_flag = rrc_exists
		}

		days = 2

#RFM rebuild #RRC
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.1005 #重建[RRC.GetName]？
	title = rcmjapan.1005.t
	desc = rcmjapan.1005.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_new_reorganized_national_government

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			1015 = {
				is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
				#is_owned_by = JAP
			}
			608 = {
				is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
				#is_owned_by = JAP
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = ROOT.subjects
				exists = yes
				is_rrc = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = no_rebuild_RRC
		}
		has_global_flag = rrc_exists
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {#YES
		name = rcmjapan.1005.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RRC_annex
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:RCM_RRC_puppet = {				
				if = {
					limit = {
						609 = { #east hebei
							is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
						}
					}
					609 = {
						PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV }
						set_state_province_controller = {
							controller = PREV
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = JAP
									tag = JAP
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#transfer_state = 609
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						613 = { #shanghai
							is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
						}
					}
					613 = {
						PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV }
						set_state_province_controller = {
							controller = PREV
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = JAP
									tag = JAP
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#transfer_state = 613
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1078 = { #shanghai
							is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
						}
					}
					1078 = {
						PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV }
						set_state_province_controller = {
							controller = PREV
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = JAP
									tag = JAP
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#transfer_state = 1078
				}
				if = { #potential capital, transfer without full control
					limit = {
						1015 = {
							is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
							#is_owned_by = JAP
						}
					}					
					1015 = {
						PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV }
						set_state_province_controller = {
							controller = PREV
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = JAP
									tag = JAP
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#transfer_state = 1015
				}
				if = { #potential capital, transfer without full control
					limit = {
						608 = {
							is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
							#is_owned_by = JAP
						}
					}
					608 = {
						PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV }
						set_state_province_controller = {
							controller = PREV
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = JAP
									tag = JAP
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#transfer_state = 608
				}
				RRC_CREATION = yes
				get_current_government_type = yes
				JAP = {
					puppet = event_target:RCM_RRC_puppet
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				
			}
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				event_target:RCM_RRC_puppet = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = JAP
						enemy = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#option = {#NO
	#	name = rcmjapan.1005.b
	#}
	option = {#NO FOREVER
		name = rcmjapan.1005.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = no_rebuild_RRC
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.1022 #[EHB.GetName]的命运
	title = rcmjapan.1022.t
	desc = rcmjapan.1022.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_new_reorganized_national_government
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #Give EHB to HPC
		name = rcmjapan.1022.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ai = yes
				HPC = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
		}
		trigger =  {
			EHB = {
				is_puppet_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					is_ai = no
					CHI = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "None" ruling_only = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		EHB = {	
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.small_china
				tooltip = small_china_tt
				add_core_of = PREV
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_claim_by = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.small_china = This.id } }
					}
					add_claim_by = PREV
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = EYW_jap_chi
			CHI = {
				get_current_government_type_global = yes
			}
			restore_previous_government_type_global = yes
			
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = democratic }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CPG
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = democratic
						name = CHI_n_socialism_cdl
						long_name = CHI_n_socialism_cdl_long
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = n_socialism }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = n_socialism
						name = CHI_communism_party_POW
						long_name = CHI_communism_party_POW_long
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = communism }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_leader_communism
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = communism
						name = PRG_party
						long_name = PRG_party_long
					}
				}
			}
		}		
		CHI = { country_event = rcmjapan.1020 }
		HPC = { country_event = rcmjapan.1020 }
	}
	option = { #Give EHB to HPC
		name = rcmjapan.1022.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ai = yes
				EHB = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ai = yes
				CHI = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "None" ruling_only = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger =  {
			HPC = {
				is_puppet_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					is_ai = no
					CHI = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "None" ruling_only = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		HPC = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.small_china
				tooltip = small_china_tt
				add_core_of = PREV
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_claim_by = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.small_china = This.id } }
					}
					add_claim_by = PREV
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = EYW_jap_chi
			CHI = {
				get_current_government_type_global = yes
			}
			restore_previous_government_type_global = yes
			
						
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = democratic }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CPG
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = democratic
						name = CHI_n_socialism_cdl
						long_name = CHI_n_socialism_cdl_long
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = n_socialism }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = n_socialism
						name = CHI_communism_party_POW
						long_name = CHI_communism_party_POW_long
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = communism }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_leader_communism
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = communism
						name = PRG_party
						long_name = PRG_party_long
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CHI = { country_event = rcmjapan.1021 }
		EHB = { country_event = rcmjapan.1021 }
	}
	option = { # Give EHB to China
		name = rcmjapan.1022.c
		trigger = { NOT = { CHI = { has_country_leader = { name = "None" ruling_only = yes } } } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				HPC = { is_puppet_of = ROOT is_ai = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				EHB = { is_puppet_of = ROOT is_ai = no }
			}
		}
		trigger =  { CHI = { is_puppet_of = ROOT } }
		CHI = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = communism
						has_government = n_socialism
					}	
				}
				load_focus_tree = warlord_generic_communist
			}
			else = {
				load_focus_tree = warlord_generic_nationalist
			}
		}
		HPC = { country_event = rcmjapan.1020 }
		EHB = { country_event = rcmjapan.1020 }
	}
}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

			country_exists = NSG
			country_exists = SCG
		}
		SCG = {
			country_event = {
				hours = 1 id = rcmjapan.91
			}
		}
		NSG = {
			country_event = {
				hours = 5 id = rcmjapan.92
			}
		}
		create_mengjiang = yes
	}
	option = {#ONE EXIST
		name = rcmjapan.90.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = NSG
				country_exists = SCG
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = NSG
					country_exists = SCG
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SCG
			}
			transfer_state = 1013
			create_mengjiang = yes
			SCG = {
				country_event = {
					hours = 1 id = rcmjapan.91
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = NSG
			}
			transfer_state = 611
			create_mengjiang = yes
			NSG = {
				country_event = {
					hours = 5 id = rcmjapan.92
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#NONE EXIST
		name = rcmjapan.90.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					country_exists = NSG
					country_exists = SCG
				}
			}
		}
		transfer_state = 1013
		transfer_state = 611
		create_mengjiang = yes
	}
}

				annex_country = {

				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = scg_exists
			clr_global_flag = nsg_exists

		}

	}

#NSG
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.99 #成立[NSG.GetName]？
	title = rcmjapan.99.t
	desc = rcmjapan.99.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NSG
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		OR = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_legit_china = yes
			}
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = mej_exists
				has_global_flag = nsg_no_puppet
				country_exists = NSG
			}
		}
		1013 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
			#is_owned_by = JAP
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.99.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NSG_establish_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = nsg_exists
			NSG = {
				transfer_state = 1013
				add_state_core = 1013
			}
			JAP = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = NSG
					autonomous_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_protectorate
				}
			}
			NSG = {
				set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
				set_political_party = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 35 }
				set_political_party = { ideology = fascism popularity = 65 }
				set_political_party = { ideology = communism popularity = 0 }
				set_political_party = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0 }
				set_political_party = { ideology = n_socialism popularity = 0 }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = GER
					modifier = GER_wuxuzaiyi
				}				
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "GER"
					value = -100
				}				
			}
			GER = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = NSG
					modifier = GER_wuxuzaiyi
				}				
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "NSG"
					value = -100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No need for that."
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = scg_no_puppet
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.105 #击垮共产党游击队！
	title = rcmjapan.105.t
	desc = rcmjapan.105.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			country_exists = PRC
		}
		OR = {
			is_subject_of = JAP
			tag = JAP
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			has_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.105.a
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = 0.05
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = remove_com_par_act_tt
			clr_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = i_cracked_down_on_you

		}
	}
}

#new colony
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.106 #一个新殖民政府成立了
	title = rcmjapan.106.t
	desc = rcmjapan.106.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.106.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = MAN
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MAN_JAP
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				#create_country_leader = {
				#	name = "Zheng Xiaoxu"
				#	picture = "Portrait_MAN_Zheng_Xiaoxu.dds"
				#	expire = "1960.1.1"
				#	ideology = moderatism
				#	traits = {
				#		staunch_monarchist
				#	}
				#}
				retire_country_leader = yes
				zheng_xiaoxu = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = moderatism
							traits = {
							}
						} 
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = staunch_monarchist
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ECA
				has_global_flag = ECA_MAF_exist

			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = ECA_MAF
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = mej_exists
				tag = ECA
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MEJ
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ECA
				has_global_flag = mua_exists
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MUA
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ECA
				has_global_flag = men_exists

			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MEN
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SIK
			}
			kill_country_leader = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = XSM
				has_government = neutrality
			}			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "XSM_ma_hongbin"
				desc = "POLITICS_MA_HONGBIN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/NXM/Portrait_NXM_Ma_Hongbin.dds"
				expire = "1952.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
				}
			}
			
			set_cosmetic_tag = XSM_HUI
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = XSM
				has_government = n_socialism
			}			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "XSM_ma_hongbin"
				desc = "POLITICS_MA_HONGBIN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/NXM/Portrait_NXM_Ma_Hongbin.dds"
				expire = "1952.1.1"
				ideology = n_authoritarian_socialism
				traits = {
				}
			}			
			set_cosmetic_tag = XSM_HUI
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				has_government = democratic
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shen_Junru"
				desc = "POLITICS_Shen_Junru_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Shen_Junru.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = n_democratic_socialism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_rrc = yes
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chen_Gongbo"
				desc = "POLITICS_WANG_JINGWEI_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Chen_Gongbo.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_rrc = yes
				has_government = n_socialism
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chen_Gongbo"
				desc = "POLITICS_WANG_JINGWEI_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Chen_Gongbo.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = n_authoritarian_socialism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = n_socialism
					}
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.4
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}

			FROM = {
				country_event = rcmjapan.1061
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = n_socialism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = n_socialism
				popularity = 0.4
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = rcmjapan.1062
			}
		}
		add_ideas = reformed_colonial_administration
	}
}

		name = wtt_japan.1.a

			base = 10
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = MAL
					tag = SST
					tag = FIC
					tag = INS
					tag = BOR
					tag = SAR	
				}
				is_puppet_of = ROOT
			}
			set_country_flag = Pacific_gaurdian_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = FIC
				}
				release = CAM
				release = VIN
				release = LAO
				FROM = {
					puppet = CAM
					puppet = VIN
					puppet = LAO
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					puppet = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcmjapan.109 days = 1 } }
	}

	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcmjapan.110 days = 1 } }
	}
}

				}
			}

					}
				}

			}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan_canton.121 #广州作战
	title = rcmjapan_canton.121.t
	desc = rcmjapan_canton.121.d

    trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
		original_tag = JAP
		surrender_progress < 0.01
		608 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
		}
		716 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
		}
		328 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
		}
		any_enemy_country = {
			owns_state = 592
		}
		592 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = no
		}
		date > 1938.10.1
		date < 1940.1.1
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers

				limit = { NOT = { controls_state = 592 }}

					limit = {

country_event = { #Motion of no confidence
	id = rcmjapan.122 #动议不信任投票
	title = rcmjapan.122.t
	desc = rcmjapan.122.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_public_hearing_2
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan.1"}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.122.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				#always = yes
				has_country_flag = RCM_unrest_against_yonai_flag
			}
			clear_all_cabinet_members_JAP = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			unlock_national_focus = JAP_second_konoe_cabinet_focus
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			country_event = rcmjapan_pm.9
			add_popularity = {
			    ideology = fascism
			    popularity = 0.4
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				name = JAP_fascism_party_tai
				long_name = JAP_fascism_party_tai
			}
			add_ideas = new_order
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_bad
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_good
					remove_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_bad
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_good
					remove_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_interservice_rivalry_navy_dominant
					add_idea = JAP_interservice_rivalry_army_dominant
				}
			}			
			clr_country_flag = RCM_unrest_against_yonai_flag
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RCM_pro_axis_unrest_YONAI_flag
			}
			clear_all_cabinet_members_JAP = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			unlock_national_focus = JAP_second_konoe_cabinet_focus
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			country_event = rcmjapan_pm.9
			add_popularity = {
			    ideology = fascism
			    popularity = 0.4
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				name = JAP_fascism_party_tai
				long_name = JAP_fascism_party_tai
			}
			add_ideas = new_order
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_bad
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_good
					remove_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_bad
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_good
					remove_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_interservice_rivalry_navy_dominant
					add_idea = JAP_interservice_rivalry_army_dominant
				}
			}	
			clr_country_flag = RCM_pro_axis_unrest_YONAI_flag
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RCM_pro_axis_unrest_KONOE_flag
			}
			clear_all_cabinet_members_JAP = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			if = {
				limit = {
					sign_triparti_pact_bypass_trigger = yes
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 988
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							is_subject_of = GER
							AND = {
								original_tag = FRA
								has_government = fascism
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						days = 20 id = rcmjapan.107
					}
				}
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 2
					name = southern_expansion
				}

				FIC = { country_event = rcmindochina.13 }

				hidden_effect = {
					news_event = {
						hours = 6
						id = news.208
					}
					USA = {
						country_event = {
							days = 15
							id = rcmjapan.9932 #日本入侵法属印度支那
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
					}
					unlock_decision_category_tooltip = prospect_for_resources
				}
				unlock_national_focus = southern_expansion_focus
				custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						sign_triparti_pact_bypass_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = fascism
					}
					country_event = {
						id = wtt_japan.109
						days = 1
					}
				}
				unlock_national_focus = JAP_sign_tripartite_pact
				custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			}
			set_country_flag = tojo_cabinet_flag
			country_event = rcmjapan_pm.11
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = hideki_tojo
			}
		}
	}

	id = rcmjapan_leave_lnc.1 #军官们要求退出《伦敦海军条约》
	title = rcmjapan_leave_lnc.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_leave_lnc.1.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_leave_lnc.1.a

			base = 100
			modifier = {
				add = -100
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_TREATY_FACTION
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_STATE_SOCIALISM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_COMMUNISM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_TOHOKAI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT
		add_stability = 0.05
		#add_political_power = -50
		remove_naval_treaty_effect = yes
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_naval_treaty_trigger = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = MTG_naval_treaty.7 days = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = {
					flag = MTG_naval_treaty_signatories
					value < 3
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_naval_treaty_trigger = yes
				}
				remove_naval_treaty_effect = yes
			}
			clr_global_flag = MTG_naval_treaty_signatories
			hidden_effect = { news_event = mtg_news.60 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MTG_naval_treaty_signatories
			}
			modify_global_flag = {
				flag = MTG_naval_treaty_signatories
				value = -1
			}
		}
		
	}

	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_leave_lnc.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = no
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_TREATY_FACTION
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_STATE_SOCIALISM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_COMMUNISM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_TOHOKAI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = 50
		set_country_flag = okada_stronk
		custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_japan_okada_stays_tt
	}

					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
				}
			}

			random_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = CPG
				load_focus_tree = warlord_generic_nationalist
				save_global_event_target_as = CDL_JAP_puppet
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
						}
					}
					event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
						PREV = {
							add_to_war = {
								targeted_alliance = JAP
								enemy = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}

				JAP = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = WTT_current_china_leader.core_states
					THIS = {
						add_core_of = event_target:CDL_JAP_puppet
					}
				}
				get_current_government_type = yes
				JAP = {
					puppet = event_target:CDL_JAP_puppet
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				create_country_leader = {
					name = Zhang_Lan
					desc = "POLITICS_ZHANG_LAN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_China_Zhang_Lan.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = socialism
					traits = {
						#
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = shanghai_will_be_CDL
	}
}

add_namespace = rcmjapan_christian
#Church athority endorsed
country_event = { 
	id = rcmjapan_christian.1 #教会影响力增加！
	title = rcmjapan_christian.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_christian.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_church_2
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				scoped_sound_effect = long_choir
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian.1.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_1
				add_idea = jap_church_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_2
				add_idea = jap_church_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_3
				add_idea = jap_church_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_4
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_4
				add_idea = jap_church_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_5
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_5
				add_idea = jap_church_6
			}
		}
	}
}
#Church authority challenged
country_event = { 
	id = rcmjapan_christian.2 #教会当局受到挑战
	title = rcmjapan_christian.2.t
	desc = rcmjapan_christian.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_asian_unrest_2
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_completed_focus = JAP_fund_the_unitarian_church_focus
		OR = {
			has_idea = jap_church_2
			has_idea = jap_church_3
			has_idea = jap_church_4
			has_idea = jap_church_5
			has_idea = jap_church_6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_2
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_10 #it's actually smaller than, but this won't be seen
				check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance < 10 }
			}				
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_3
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_30 #it's actually smaller than, but this won't be seen
				check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance < 30 }
			}				
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_4
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_50 #it's actually smaller than, but this won't be seen
				check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance < 50 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_5
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_70 #it's actually smaller than, but this won't be seen
				check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance < 70 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_6
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_90 #it's actually smaller than, but this won't be seen
				check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance < 90 }
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian.2.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_6
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_6
				add_idea = jap_church_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_5
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_5
				add_idea = jap_church_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_4
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_4
				add_idea = jap_church_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_3
				add_idea = jap_church_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = jap_church_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = jap_church_2
				add_idea = jap_church_1
			}
		}
		
	}
}

	title = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_support_small.6.t
	desc = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_support_small.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_shinto_shrine
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_support_small.6.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = add_3_support_point
		282 = {
			add_to_variable = {
				This.Local_christian_acceptance = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash
#996 Tokachi backlash
country_event = { 
	id = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1 #十胜反对新宗教迫害禁令
	title = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_asian_unrest_2
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
		996 = {
			set_state_flag = This_state_has_backlash
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1.a
		trigger = {
			always = no #this cause bugs, player can use decision later
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		996 = {
			save_global_event_target_as = pacify_christian_state
		}
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
			activate_mission = RCM_send_in_the_garrison_mission
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
	}
}

	id = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_support_small.8 #东海对宗教自由的新宪法修正案兴趣缺缺
	title = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_support_small.8.t
	desc = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_support_small.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_shinto_shrine
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_support_small.8.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = add_3_support_point
		532 = {
			add_to_variable = {
				This.Local_christian_acceptance = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash
#996 Tokachi backlash
country_event = { 
	id = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1 #十胜反对有关宗教自由的新宪法修正案
	title = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1.d
	picture = report_event_asian_unrest_2
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
		996 = {
			set_state_flag = This_state_has_backlash
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1.a
		trigger = {
			always = no #this cause bugs, player can use decision later
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		996 = {
			save_global_event_target_as = pacify_christian_state
		}
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
			activate_mission = RCM_send_in_the_garrison_mission
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
	}
}

#season start news
news_event = {
	id = rcmjapan_baseball_news.1 #两年一度的东京Big6棒球赛开始了！
	title = rcmjapan_baseball_news.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_baseball_news.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_baseball_opening
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ROOT = {
				sound_effect = baseball_1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = stake_level_1 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = stake_level_2 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = stake_level_3 }
			}
			set_country_flag = stake_level_1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball_news.1.a		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opt_out_of_baseball_bets }
			}
			country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.1
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

			has_country_flag = I_won_this_match_champion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball_news.2.c

		}
	}
}

	id = rcmjapan_baseball.1 #新一季的校际棒球比赛即将开始！
	title = rcmjapan_baseball.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_baseball.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stadium
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		clr_baseball_game_data = yes
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = opt_out_of_baseball_bets
		}
	}
	option = { #intro
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.1.a
		country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.2	
	}
	option = { #skip to choosing
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.1.b
		country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.8	
	}
	option = { #opt out of bets
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.1.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = opt_out_of_baseball_bets_tt
		set_country_flag = opt_out_of_baseball_bets
		set_country_flag = autorun_on
		activate_mission = RCM_JAP_game_in_progress_no_champion_mission
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = civies_finished_last_low_stake
			}
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = civies_finished_last_mid_stake
			}
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = civies_finished_last_high_stake
			}
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = This.reward_civ }
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

			has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 200
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = JAP_ai_behavior 
					option = OKADA_STAYS_COMMUNISM
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = rcmjapan_left_reform_a_tt

			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.08
		}

		MAN = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = n_socialism
				popularity = -0.03
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.03
			}
			add_manpower = -5000
			country_event = rcmjapan_left_reform.2

		}
	}

				factor = 200

				}
			}
		}

			remove_ideas = strikes_1
			clr_country_flag = crisis_in_progress
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_left_reform.1.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = rcmjapan_left_reform_c_tt

			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 200
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = JAP_ai_behavior 
					option = OKADA_STAYS_TOHOKAI
				}
			}

#Japans asks to take overlordship if country has capitulated
country_event = {
	id = wtt_japan.1 #[From.GetNameDefCap]要求接管我国殖民地
	title = wtt_japan.1.t
	desc = wtt_japan.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Accept transfer puppet
	#Checking for puppet in decision that fires event.
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { tag = HOL }
			}
			FROM = { puppet = INS }
		}

		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { tag = ENG }
			}
			FROM = { puppet = MAL }
		}

		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { tag = FRA } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					670 = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = FRA
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = 670 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					988 = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = FRA
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = 988 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					286 = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = FRA
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = 286 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					741 = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = FRA
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = 741 }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = wtt_japan.2 days = 1 } }
	}

	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = wtt_japan.3 days = 1 } }
	}
}

 # Event for Germany to accept Tripartite Pact
country_event = {
	id = wtt_japan.109 #日本提议缔结三国同盟条约
	title = wtt_japan.109.t
	desc = wtt_japan.109.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_europe_pact

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = { save_event_target_as = JAP_initiator }
			save_event_target_as = GER_fascism
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ITA
					has_government = fascism
				}
				save_event_target_as = ITA_fascism
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.109.a #accept
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}

		event_target:ITA_fascism = {
			country_event = { id = wtt_japan.110 hours = 6 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.109.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		event_target:JAP_initiator = { country_event = { id = wtt_japan.112 hours = 6 } }
		event_target:ITA_fascism = { country_event = { id = wtt_japan.112 hours = 6 } }
	}
}

		        type = befriend

	        }

		        type = befriend

	            }
			}

		        type = befriend
		        id = GER
		        value = 200
	        }

		        type = befriend

#Democratic Coup event
country_event = {
	id = wtt_japan.114 #民主派发动政变
	title = wtt_japan.114.t
	desc = wtt_japan.114.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_soldiers_02

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.114.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				MAN = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			set_autonomy = { target = MAN autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			if = {
				limit = {
					MEN = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
				MAN = { puppet = MEN }
			}
			MAN = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = MAN_kwantung_army
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MAN = { has_idea = MAN_kwantung_veto }
			}
			MAN = { remove_ideas = MAN_kwantung_veto }
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.1 }
		start_civil_war = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			ideology = fascism
			size = 0.5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_controlled_state = { #MODDED
					is_core_of = KOR
				}
			}
			release = KOR
			set_autonomy = { target = KOR autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
		}
	}
}

#German notification event that Japan has gone to war with USSR despite mol-rib pact
country_event = {
	id = wtt_japan.115 #[From.GetName]进攻苏联
	title = wtt_japan.115.t
	desc = wtt_japan.115.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_parade

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Join the war
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.115.a
		add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = JAP enemy = SOV hostility_reason = ally }
		JAP = { country_event = { id = wtt_japan.116 hours = 6 } }
	}

	# Keep the NAP
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.115.b
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = unilateral_war }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = betrayed_alliance }
		JAP = { country_event = { id = wtt_japan.117 hours = 6 } }
	}
}

# Event for MAN: Commie JAP took Tokyo
country_event = {
	id = wtt_japan.121 #[From.GetName]攻占东京
	title = wtt_japan.121.t
	desc = wtt_japan.121.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_army_parade

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Annex them!
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.121.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		event_target:jap_civ_loser = { delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Japanese Loyalist Regiment" } }
		FROM = {
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Japanese People's Regiment" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Soviet Volunteers" }
			transfer_state = 529
			transfer_state = 530
			transfer_state = 528
			transfer_state = 282
			transfer_state = 533
			transfer_state = 536
			transfer_state = 555
			country_event = { id = wtt_japan.122 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = { has_country_flag = sent_volunteers_to_JAP }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				SOV = { add_manpower = 105000 }
			}
			country_event = { id = wtt_japan.124 }
		}
		annex_country = { target = event_target:jap_civ_loser transfer_troops = yes }
		set_cosmetic_tag = MAN_kwantung_army
	}

	# This is not our fight.
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.121.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			annex_country = { target = event_target:jap_civ_loser }
			country_event = { id = wtt_japan.123 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = { has_country_flag = sent_volunteers_to_JAP }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				SOV = { add_manpower = 105000 }
			}
			country_event = { id = wtt_japan.124 }
		}
	}
}

# Event for China that Japan wants to surrender
country_event = {
	id = wtt_japan.126 #[From.GetName]提议和谈
	title = wtt_japan.126.t
	desc = wtt_japan.126.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_chinese_surrender

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# We accept their surrender.
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.126.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						MAN = {
							controls_state = 525
							controls_state = 527
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = { release = KOR }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					524 = {
						is_controlled_by = JAP
					}
				}
				event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
					transfer_state = 524
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { #Chinese United Front
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_literally_china = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
					}
					every_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							OWNER = {
							OR = {
									original_tag = JAP
									is_subject_of = JAP
									is_in_faction_with = JAP
								}
								}
							}
						CONTROLLER = {
							transfer_state = PREV
							}
						}
				}
				every_other_country = {
							limit = {
								is_literally_china = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
					}
					white_peace = ROOT
				}
			}
			else = {
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_literally_china = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					every_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							OWNER = {
							OR = {
									original_tag = JAP
									is_subject_of = JAP
									is_in_faction_with = JAP
								}
								}
							}
						CONTROLLER = {
							transfer_state = PREV
						}
							}
						}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_literally_china = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					white_peace = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = wtt_japan.127 }
		}
		set_country_flag = achievement_JAP_sue_for_peace_CHI_completed
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
	}

	# No surrender! We want total victory!
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.126.b
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = wtt_japan.128 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = { # If Japan has lots of major enemies, the AI will not make a separate peace
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				USA = {
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				ENG = {
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				SOV = {
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				FRA = {
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				GER = {
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				HOL = {
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				ITA = {
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Event for Japan that China has accepted
country_event = {
	id = wtt_japan.127 #[From.GetName]同意和谈
	title = wtt_japan.127.t
	desc = wtt_japan.127.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_chinese_surrender

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# They have accepted.
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.127.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					MAN = {
						controls_state = 525
						controls_state = 527
					}
				}
			}
			release = KOR
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				524 = { #Taiwan
					is_controlled_by = JAP
				}
			}
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				transfer_state = 524
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { #Chinese United Front
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				every_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
						OR = {
								original_tag = JAP
								is_subject_of = JAP
								is_in_faction_with = JAP
							}
						}
					}
					CONTROLLER = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
						}
					}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				every_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
						OR = {
								original_tag = JAP
								is_subject_of = JAP
								is_in_faction_with = JAP
							}
							}
						}
					CONTROLLER = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_literally_china = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				white_peace = ROOT
				}
			}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_truce = {
				target = PRC
				days = 730
			}
			set_truce = {
				target = CHI
				days = 730
			}
			set_truce = {
				target = XSM
				days = 730
			}
			set_truce = {
				target = SHX
				days = 730
			}
			set_truce = {
				target = GXC
				days = 730
			}
			set_truce = {
				target = YUN
				days = 730
			}
			set_truce = {
				target = SIK
				days = 730
			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 1
		}

			if = {
				limit = {
					#chi is also war with JAP, no need transfer taiwan
					event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = JAP
						}
					}
					##
					524 = {
						is_controlled_by = JAP
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 524
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = PREV
					is_owned_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = MAN
						has_war_with = FROM
						controls_state = PREV
					}
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			white_peace = FROM
			FROM = {
				release = KOR				
			}		## MODDED^^^^	
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = wtt_japan.130 }
		}
	}

		name = wtt_japan.126.b

#Japan wins
country_event = {
	id = japan_border_conflict.2 #日军取得哈桑湖之战胜利
	title = japan_border_conflict.2.t
	desc = japan_border_conflict.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = japan_border_conflict.2.a
		trigger = {
			original_tag = JAP
		}
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
             name = sov_jap_border_conflict_won
             cost_reduction = 0.5
             uses = 1
             category = land_doctrine
        }
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = sov_jap_border_conflict_won
			category = armor
			bonus = 1.0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = japan_border_conflict.2.b
		trigger = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}
		army_experience = 20
	}
}
